\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em This function allows you to replace the default log output function with one of your own. \end{DoxyCompactList}\end{DoxyCompactItemize}


\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Simple log messages with categories and priorities.

By default logs are quiet, but if you\textquotesingle{}re debugging S\+DL you might want\+: \begin{DoxyVerb}SDL_LogSetAllPriority(SDL_LOG_PRIORITY_WARN);
\end{DoxyVerb}


Here\textquotesingle{}s where the messages go on different platforms\+: Windows\+: debug output stream Android\+: log output Others\+: standard error output (stderr)

\doxysubsection{Enumeration Type Documentation}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{anonymous enum}{anonymous enum}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily anonymous enum}



The predefined log categories. 

By default the application category is enabled at the I\+N\+FO level, the assert category is enabled at the W\+A\+RN level, test is enabled at the V\+E\+R\+B\+O\+SE level and all other categories are enabled at the C\+R\+I\+T\+I\+C\+AL level. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
